<script type="text/javascript">
    var checkLoadTaboola = false;
    if (!checkLoadTaboola) {
        let body = document.querySelector('body');
        function loadTaboola() {
            if(!checkLoadTaboola){
                $.get('/main/get_taboola',function(res){
                    $(".load-taboola").html(res);
                });
                checkLoadTaboola = true;
            }
        }

        body.addEventListener('mouseover',
            loadTaboola,
            false
        );

        document.addEventListener('scroll',
            loadTaboola,
            false
        );

        setTimeout(function(){ 
            body.addEventListener('mouseover', function () {
                body.removeEventListener('mouseover',
                    loadTaboola,
                    false
                );
            });

            document.addEventListener('scroll', function () {
                document.removeEventListener('scroll',
                    loadTaboola,
                    false
                );
            });
        }, 3000);
    }
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    document.addEventListener("click", function(){
        var itemMenus = document.querySelectorAll('.common-site-links .menu-item .dropdown-site-link ');
        itemMenus.forEach(function(iElement){
            iElement.style.display = "none";
            iElement.parentNode.classList.remove("active");
        });
    });

    var clickElements = document.querySelectorAll('.common-site-links .has-dropdown');
    clickElements.forEach(function(element){
        element.addEventListener("click",(e)=>{
            e.preventDefault();
            e.stopPropagation();
            

            if(e.currentTarget.parentNode.classList.contains('active')){
                e.currentTarget.parentNode.querySelector('.dropdown-site-link').style.display = "none";
                e.currentTarget.parentNode.classList.remove("active");
            }else{
                e.currentTarget.parentNode.querySelector('.dropdown-site-link').style.display = "block";
                e.currentTarget.parentNode.classList.add("active");
            }
        })
    });
    clickElements.forEach(function(element){
        element.addEventListener("blur",(e)=>{
            if(!e.relatedTarget || e.relatedTarget.className != "d-flex align-items-center px-3 py-2"){
                var test  = document.querySelectorAll('.common-site-links .menu-item .dropdown-site-link a');
                var itemMenus = document.querySelectorAll('.common-site-links .menu-item .dropdown-site-link');
                itemMenus.forEach(function(iElement){
                    iElement.style.display = "none";
                });
                var menuItems = document.querySelectorAll('.common-site-links .menu-item');
                menuItems.forEach(function(iElement){
                    iElement.classList.remove("active");
                });
            }
            if(e.relatedTarget && e.relatedTarget.className === "d-flex align-items-center px-3 py-2"){
                setTimeout(()=>{
                    var itemMenus = document.querySelectorAll('.common-site-links .menu-item .dropdown-site-link');
                    itemMenus.forEach(function(iElement){
                        iElement.style.display = "none";
                    });
                },300)
            }
            
        });
        var itemMenus = document.querySelectorAll('.common-site-links .menu-item .dropdown-site-link ');
        itemMenus.forEach(function(iElement){
                iElement.style.display = "none";
            });
    });
    
    var $hd_txt_ad = Math.floor(Math.random() * Math.floor(3));
    if ($hd_txt_ad === 0) {
        document.querySelector(".common-site-links .link-site-affiliate").innerHTML= ('<a style="color: #D73A4E;" class="p-2 d-flex h-100" href="https://www.ac-illust.com/creator/resist.html" target="_blank">イラストを投稿しませんか？</a>');
    } else if ($hd_txt_ad === 1) {
        document.querySelector(".common-site-links .link-site-affiliate").innerHTML= ('<a style="color: #D73A4E;" class="p-2 d-flex h-100" href="https://www.photo-ac.com/creator/auth/register" target="_blank">あなたも写真を投稿しませんか？</a>');
    } else {
        document.querySelector(".common-site-links .link-site-affiliate").innerHTML= ('<a style="color: #D73A4E;" class="p-2 d-flex h-100" href="https://www.ac-associate.com/" target="_blank">ご紹介で100円の広告報酬！</a>');
    }
</script></div>

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(".menu-top-toggler").click(function(){
        var target = $(this).data('target');
        $(target).addClass('active');
    })
    jQuery(document).on('click', function(e) {
        $("#menu-top-dropdown").removeClass('active');
    });
    jQuery(document).on('click', function(e) {
        $(".close-menu-top").removeClass('active');
    });
    jQuery(document).on('click', "#menu-top-dropdown .navbar-nav, .menu-top-toggler", function(e) {
        e.stopPropagation();
    });
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    function showMobileInfoSidebar() {
        var mobileInfoSidebar = $("#mb-info-sidebar");
        var overlayFilter = $("#overlay-filter");
        $("body").css('overflow', 'hidden');
        mobileInfoSidebar.addClass('active').show();
        overlayFilter.show();
    }
    function clearOverlay() {
        var mobileFilterFixed = $("#filter-horizontal");
        var mobileFilterSearch = $("#ac-navigation-left");
        var mobileInfoSidebar = $("#mb-info-sidebar");
        var overlayFilter = $("#overlay-filter");
        $("body").css('overflow', 'visible');
        mobileFilterFixed.removeClass('active');
        mobileFilterSearch.removeClass('active');
        mobileInfoSidebar.removeClass('active').hide();
        overlayFilter.hide();
    }
</script>                    </div>

<script type="text/javascript">
	$('.search-form-d select#age').on('change', function(){
		let val_seletecd = this.value;
		if($(".search-form-d .coll-8 input[type='radio'][name='model_count']:checked").val() == '0' && val_seletecd != 'all'){
			$('.search-form-d .mdlrlrsec_1').trigger('click');
		}
	})

	$(".search-form-d .coll-8 input[type='radio'][name='model_count']").on('change', function(){
		let val_checked = this.value;
		if(val_checked == 0){
			$('.search-form-d select#age').val('all').change();
		}
	})
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    $('.search-box-top-fixed-area select#age').on('change', function(){
		let val_seletecd = this.value;
		if($(".search-box-top-fixed-area .coll-88 input[type='radio'][name='model_count']:checked").val() == '0' && val_seletecd != 'all'){
			$('.search-box-top-fixed-area .mdlrlrsec_1').trigger('click');
		}
	})

    $('#search-form-wrap input[name=q]').on('input', function(){
		$("#search-form-wrap .clone-sw").text(this.value);
		addjustFilterFieldPosition("#search-form-wrap");
	})

    $('#search-form-fixed-wrap input[name=q]').on('input', function(){
		$("#search-form-fixed-wrap .clone-sw").text(this.value);
		addjustFilterFieldPosition("#search-form-fixed-wrap");
	})

	$(".search-box-top-fixed-area .coll-88 input[type='radio'][name='model_count']").on('change', function(){
		let val_checked = this.value;
		if(val_checked == 0){
			$('.search-box-top-fixed-area select#age').val('all').change();
		}
	})

	function showResetKeywordsButton(_this) {
    	var parentSelector = _this.parents('form');
    	if (_this.val()) {
    		setPositionKeywordsButton(_this);
    		parentSelector.find('.reset-keywords-btn').show();
    	} else {
    		parentSelector.find('.reset-keywords-btn').hide();
    	}
    }

    function setPositionKeywordsButton(_this) {
    	var parentSelector = _this.parents('form');
    	var position = parentSelector.find('.search-file').outerWidth() + parentSelector.find('#advsearchbtn').outerWidth() + parentSelector.find('.execloginbtn').outerWidth();
    	parentSelector.find('.reset-keywords-btn').css({right: position});
    }

	function showTopSearchBar(){
		$(".search-box-top-fixed-area").show();
		$(".sticky-search .flex-grow-1.ac-mr-xl-3.mt-2.mt-xl-0").hide();
		setPositionKeywordsButton($(".search-box-top-fixed-area .search-box-top-fixed input[name='q']"));
	}

	function hideTopSearchBar(){
		$(".search-box-top-fixed-area").hide();
		$(".sticky-search .flex-grow-1.ac-mr-xl-3.mt-2.mt-xl-0").show();
		$(".search-box-top-fixed .search-box").removeClass('has-triangle');
		$(".search-box-top-fixed-area .advsearcharea").hide();
	}
	
	$(document).ready(function(){
		$(window).on('load resize scroll', function() {
			var y_scroll_pos = window.pageYOffset;
			var sticky_position = 0;
			var filter_position = 0;
			var search_position = 0;
		
			if ($('#search-top-box').length >= 1 ) {
				search_position = $('#search-top-box').offset().top;
			}
		
			if ($('#filter-horizontal').length >= 1 ) {
				filter_position = $('#filter-horizontal').offset().top;
			}
		
			if ($('.sticky-search').length >= 1 ) {
				sticky_position = $('.sticky-search').offset().top;
			}

			if(y_scroll_pos > sticky_position && $(window).width() > 991) {
				showTopSearchBar();
			} else if (y_scroll_pos > search_position && $(window).width() < 992) {
				showTopSearchBar();
			} else {
				hideTopSearchBar();
			}

			if(y_scroll_pos > filter_position - 50) {
				$('#filter-horizontal').addClass('ac-z-index-999');
			} else {
				$('#filter-horizontal').removeClass('ac-z-index-999');
			}

			if(y_scroll_pos > filter_position - 15) {
				$('#filter-horizontal').addClass('custom-shadow');
			} else {
				$('#filter-horizontal').removeClass('custom-shadow');
			}
		});
	});
	
	function addjustFilterFieldPosition(selector){
		var currentSelector = $(selector);
    	const adjust_filter_field = currentSelector.find(".adjust-filter-field");
    	
    	const search_box_w = currentSelector.outerWidth();
    	const input_w = currentSelector.find("input[name='q']").outerWidth();
    	const button1_w = currentSelector.find(".search-file").outerWidth();
    	const button2_w = currentSelector.find("#advsearchbtn").outerWidth();
    	const button3_w = currentSelector.find(".execloginbtn").outerWidth();
    	const button4_w = currentSelector.find("#showFilterSearch").outerWidth();
    	const clone_input_w = currentSelector.find(".clone-sw").outerWidth();

    	if (clone_input_w > 0) {
    		adjust_filter_field.css('left', clone_input_w + 32);
			adjust_filter_field.css('width', search_box_w - (button1_w + button3_w) - (clone_input_w + 48));
    	} else {
    		adjust_filter_field.css('left', 172);
			adjust_filter_field.css('width', search_box_w - (button1_w + button3_w) - 188);    		
    	}
	    adjust_filter_field.css('opacity', 1);
	}

    $(window).on('resize load', function() {
    	addjustFilterFieldPosition("#search-form-fixed-wrap");
    	addjustFilterFieldPosition("#search-form-wrap");
    });

    function trimAdvsearchareaText(selector){
		selector.change(function(){
			var creator_val = $(this).val();
			$(this).val(creator_val.trim());
		});
	}

	$(document).ready(function(){
		trimAdvsearchareaText($(".advsearcharea input[type='text']"));
	});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    var activatedClass = 'omega-activated';

    $(document).on('click','.btn-show-sp-menu',function(e){
        e.preventDefault;
        $("#omega-menu").addClass(activatedClass);
    });

    $(document).on('keydown','.btn-show-sp-menu',function(e){
        e.preventDefault;
        if($("#omega-menu").hasClass(activatedClass)){
            if (e.which === 27){
                $("#omega-menu").removeClass(activatedClass);
            }
        }
    });

    $(document).on('click','#omega-overlay, .btn-mobile-close',function(e){
        e.preventDefault;
        $("#omega-menu").removeClass(activatedClass);
    });
</script>

<script>
var isImageSearchLoading = false;
var isFileInputClicked = false;
getUploadURL = ({fileName, contentType}) => {
    const params = {
        files: [{
            filename: fileName,
            content_type: contentType,
        }]
    };
    return fetch('https://upload.compressor-ac.net/upload-url', {
        method: 'POST',
        mode: 'cors',
        headers: {
            'Content-Type': 'application/json',
        },
        body: JSON.stringify(params)
    }).then(res => res.json());
};

uploadImage = async (fileObj) => {
    const presignedData = await this.getUploadURL({
        fileName: fileObj.name,
        contentType: fileObj.type,
    });
    await fetch(presignedData[0].upload_url, {
        method: 'PUT',
        mode: 'cors',
        headers: {
            'Content-Type': fileObj.type,
        },
        body: fileObj,
    });
    return {
        original_url: presignedData[0].original_url
    }
};
function uploadImageAjax(file) {
	
		var errorMessage = undefined;
		if (file != undefined) {
			var acceptType = ['jpeg', 'jpg', 'png'];
			if (-1 == $.inArray(file.type.split('/')[1], acceptType)) {
				errorMessage = 'エラーが発生しました。ファイル形式を確認してください。';
			} else if (file.size > 5 * 1024 * 1024) {
				errorMessage = 'アップロードできる画像サイズは5MBまでです。';
			}
		} else {
			errorMessage = 'エラーが発生しました。ファイル形式を確認してください。';
		}
		if (errorMessage != undefined) {
			$(".wrap-upload-file").css('background','#fff');
			alert(errorMessage);
			return false;
		}
		var sndRec = {
			token_org: 'cR5myPfi'
		};

		$.ajax( {
			url: "/ajax/public/is_enable_search",
			type: "POST",
			data: sndRec,
			dataType: 'json',
			timeout: 10000,
			success: function(response, sts, xhr) {
				if ( response.status != "success" ) {
					$("#uploadFile").modal('hide');
					$("#searchLimitModal").modal('show');
				} else {
                    $('.wrap-upload-file').find('li').hide();
                    $('#preloader').show();
                    if (file) {
                        let fr = new FileReader;
                        fr.readAsDataURL(file);
                        fr.onload = async function() {
                            if (!isImageSearchLoading) {
                                isImageSearchLoading = true;
                                const data = await uploadImage(file);
                                url = new URL(data.original_url);
                                url = url.pathname;
                                url = url.substring(1, url.length);
                                url = encodeURIComponent(url);
                                window.location.href = '/search/ris?object_id=' + url;
                            }
                        };
                    }
                }
			},
			error: function(e) {
				alert("通信エラーです。もう一度お試しください。");
				return false;
			}
		} );

}
$('#files').on('change', function (e){
	e.preventDefault();
	$('.wrap-upload-file').css('background','#e6e6e6');
	let file = $("input[type='file']")[0].files[0];
	if (isFileInputClicked) {
		uploadImageAjax(file);
	}
});
$(".wrap-upload-file").on("dragover", function(event) {
    event.preventDefault();  
	event.stopPropagation();
	$(this).css('background','#e6e6e6');
});

$(".wrap-upload-file").on("dragleave", function(event) {
    event.preventDefault();  
	event.stopPropagation();
	$(this).css('background','#fff');
});

$(".wrap-upload-file").on("drop", function(event) {
    event.preventDefault();  
	event.stopPropagation();
	if (event.originalEvent.dataTransfer.files) {
		uploadImageAjax(event.originalEvent.dataTransfer.files[0]);
	}
});

$('#uploadFile').on('show.bs.modal', function (e) {
	$("input[type='file']").val('');
	isFileInputClicked = false;
})

$('#files').on('click', function() {
	isFileInputClicked = true;
});

<script type="text/javascript">
    const popup_detail_url = $(".popup-detail-url");
    const popup_detail_dl_url = $(".popup-detail-dl-url");
    const popup_detail_editor_url = $(".popup-detail-editor-url"); 
    const popup_detail_add_to_cart = $(".popup-detail-add-to-cart");

    $(document).on('click', 'a[data-target="#thumbModal"]',async function(e){
        
                
        var modalTarget = '#thumbModal';
        var data_id = $(this).attr('data-id');
        var title = $(this).attr('data-title');
        var filename = $(this).attr('data-filename');
        var provider_id = $(this).attr('data-provider-id');
        var disp_flg = $(this).attr('data-disp-flg');
        var disp_type = $(this).attr('data-disp-type');
        var disp_size_downloaded = $(this).attr('data-size-downloaded');
        var safety_flg = $(this).attr('data-safety-flg');
        var sell_exl_flg = $(this).attr('data-sell-exl-flg');
        var nick_name = $(this).attr('data-nickname');
        var nice_cnt = $(this).attr('data-nice-cnt');
        var premium_only = $(this).attr('data-premium-only');
        var data_dimension_s = $(this).attr('data-dimension-s');
        var data_dimension_m = $(this).attr('data-dimension-m');
        var data_dimension_l = $(this).attr('data-dimension-l');
        var data_dimension_ps = $(this).attr('data-dimension-ps');
        var data_size_s = $(this).attr('data-size-s');
        var data_size_m = $(this).attr('data-size-m');
        var data_size_l = $(this).attr('data-size-l');
        var data_size_ps = $(this).attr('data-size-ps');
        
        var thumbnailBase = "https://thumb.photo-ac.com/";
        var subDir = filename.substr(0, 2);
        var thumbnail = thumbnailBase + subDir + '/' + filename + '_w.jpeg';
        var detailUrl = '/main/detail/' + data_id;
        var searchId = $('#searchId').attr('search-id');
        var defaultSelectedSize = disp_type == 'purchased' ? convertNumberToSize(disp_size_downloaded) : 's';
        var onclickUrl = '/main/donations/';
        var serviceURL = baseURL + "/auth/sso_login?redirect_to=" + encodeURIComponent(detailUrl);
        var loginlUrl =  SSO_SERVER_URL + "/login?serviceURL=" + encodeURIComponent(serviceURL);
        var signuplUrl =  SSO_SERVER_URL + "/signup?serviceURL=" +  encodeURIComponent(serviceURL);

        await checkCreatorBlocked(provider_id);

        $("input[name=size][value=" + defaultSelectedSize + "]").prop('checked', true);

                
        function rowSizeTooltip(value = null, type = null){
            var totalSizeType = eval('data_size_'+type) ? Math.round(100*eval('data_size_'+type)/(1024*1024))/100 : 0;
            $('#row-size-' + type).tooltip({
                trigger: 'hover',
                title: value + 'px' + ' (' + totalSizeType + 'M)',
                placement: 'bottom',
            });
        }

        function renderDimensionAndTotalSize(value = null, type = null){
            var totalSizeType = eval('data_size_'+type) ? Math.round(100*eval('data_size_'+type)/(1024*1024))/100 : 0;
            $('#dimension-size-' + type).text(value + 'px');
            $('#total-size-' + type).text(totalSizeType + 'M');
        }

        function hideRowSizePopup(value = null, type = null){
            if (value) {
                $('#row-size-' + type).show();
                                    rowSizeTooltip(value, type);
                                renderDimensionAndTotalSize(value, type);
            } else {
                $('#row-size-' + type).hide();
            }
        }

        function convertNumberToSize(size = 1){
            var result = 's';
            if (size == 2) {
                result = 'm';
            }else if (size == 3) {
                result = 'l';
            }else if (size == 4) {
                result = 'ps';
            }
            return result;
        }

        function convertSize(size = 's'){
            var result = 'small-img';
            if (size == 'm') {
                result = 'medium-img';
            }else if (size == 'l') {
                result = 'large-img';
            }else if (size == 'ps') {
                result = 'psd-img';
            }
            return result;
        }

        if(title) {
            detailUrl += '?title=' + encodeURI(title);
            if(searchId) {
                detailUrl += '&searchId=' + encodeURI(searchId);
            }
        }else if(searchId) {
            detailUrl += '?searchId=' + encodeURI(searchId);
        }

        if(provider_id == "" || disp_flg == 0){
            $('#popDetail').hide();
            $('#popDetailError').html('申し訳ございません。この写真は削除されたか、非公開に設定されました。').show();
            return false;
        } else {
            $('#popDetailError').hide();
            $('#popDetail').show();
        }

        if (data_dimension_ps) {
            $(".switch-heading").text('サイズ・形式を選択');
        } else {
            $(".switch-heading").text('形式を選択してください');            
        }

        hideRowSizePopup(data_dimension_ps, 'ps');
        hideRowSizePopup(data_dimension_l, 'l');
        hideRowSizePopup(data_dimension_m, 'm');
        hideRowSizePopup(data_dimension_s, 's');
        
        getFanPopup(provider_id);

        $('#thum img.thumb-large').attr('src', thumbnail);
        $('#modal-nickname').html(nick_name);
        $('#modal-provider-link').attr('href', '/profile/' + provider_id);
        
        $(modalTarget + ' .detail-link').attr('href', detailUrl);

        $('#modal-login-url').attr('href', loginlUrl);
        $('#modal-signup-url').attr('href', signuplUrl);
        $('#popDetail .nice-count').html(toNumberFormat(nice_cnt));

        $('#nice-btn-modal').unbind('click');
        $('#nice-btn-modal').on('click', function() {
            update_nice(data_id, null);
        });

        $('#addfan-btn-modal').unbind('click');
        $('#addfan-btn-modal').on('click', function() {
            setFanPopup(provider_id);
        });

        $("#fb-share-detail").attr('href', 'https://www.facebook.com/dialog/share?app_id=117646314917595&display=popup&href=' + encodeURIComponent(location.host + detailUrl));
        $("#pin-share-detail").attr('href', 'https://pinterest.com/pin/create/bookmarklet/?media=' + thumbnail + '&url=' + encodeURIComponent(location.host + detailUrl) + '&description=' + title + '写真素材 - No: ' + data_id + '／写真素材｜無料素材のフリーダウンロードサイト【写真AC】');
        $("#tw-share-detail").attr('href', 'https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?url=' + encodeURIComponent(location.host + detailUrl) + '&text=' + title + '&hashtags=写真AC');

                    if(disp_type == 'purchased'){
                popup_detail_url.attr({'href': '/user/order/dl/?p_id=' + data_id + '&sz=' + defaultSelectedSize + '&f=' + filename, 'target': ''});
                popup_detail_dl_url.attr({'href': '/user/order/dl/?p_id=' + data_id + '&sz=' + defaultSelectedSize + '&f=' + filename, 'target': ''});
            } else {
                if(premium_only == 1) {
                    popup_detail_url.attr('href', detailUrl + '?single_sell=1&selected_size=' + defaultSelectedSize);
                } else {
                    popup_detail_url.attr('href', detailUrl);
                }
            }
        
        $("input[name=size]").change(function() {
            var currentSelectedSize = $(this).val();
            var dlUrl = detailUrl;

            if (Array('s', 'm', 'l', 'ps').includes(currentSelectedSize)) {
                                    if (disp_type == 'purchased') {
                        popup_detail_url.attr('href', '/user/order/dl/?p_id=' + data_id + '&sz=' + currentSelectedSize + '&f=' + filename);
                        popup_detail_dl_url.attr('href', '/user/order/dl/?p_id=' + data_id + '&sz=' + currentSelectedSize + '&f=' + filename);
                    } else {
                        if(premium_only == 1) {
                            dlUrl = detailUrl + '?single_sell=1&selected_size=' + currentSelectedSize;
                        }
                        popup_detail_url.attr('href', dlUrl);
                        popup_detail_dl_url.attr('href', dlUrl);
                    }
                            }

            if (Array('s', 'm', 'l').includes(currentSelectedSize)) {
                popup_detail_editor_url.attr('href', "javascript:onDownload('" + dlUrl + "&editor=true', '" + onclickUrl + "');");
                popup_detail_editor_url.removeClass("disabled"); 
            } else {
                popup_detail_editor_url.attr('href', "javascript:void(0);");
                popup_detail_editor_url.addClass("disabled");
            }

            popup_detail_add_to_cart.unbind('click');
            popup_detail_add_to_cart.on('click', function() {
                download_select(this, data_id, title, convertSize(currentSelectedSize), filename);
            });
        });


        if (user_bookmarks) {
            var _bookmarks = JSON.parse( user_bookmarks );
            if(_bookmarks != null) {
                for ( var i=0; i<_bookmarks.length; i++ ) {
                    if ( _bookmarks[i]['data_id'] == data_id ) {
                        $('#fav-btn-modal').attr('data-execmode', 'del');
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        $('#fav-btn-modal').unbind('click');
        $('#fav-btn-modal').on('click', function() {
            var type = $(this).attr('data-execmode');
            if (type == 'add') {
                add_fav(data_id);
            } else if (type == 'del') {
                del_fav(data_id);                    
            }
        });
    });
    
    $('#thumbModal').on('hidden.bs.modal', function () {
        $('#fav-btn-modal').attr('data-execmode', 'add');
        $("input[name=size][value=s]").prop('checked', true);
    });

    function getFanPopup(provider_id = null) {
        if ( !provider_id ) return false;
        var data = {provider_id: provider_id};
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            url: '/ajax/public/get_fans_by_user',
            data: data,
            dataType: 'json',
            success: function(res){
                if(res.status == 'success')
                {
                    $('#popup-fan-count').html(toNumberFormat(res.data));
                    if (res.data == 0) {
                        $('#popup-fan-count').hide();
                    }
                }
            },
            error: function(){
            }
        });
    }

    function setFanPopup(provider_id = null) {
        if ( !provider_id ) return false;
        var data = {following: provider_id};
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            url: '/ajax/public/fan',
            data: data,
            dataType: 'json',
            success: function(res){
                if(res.status == 'success')
                {
                    var fan_count = toNumberInt($('#popup-fan-count').html());
                    $('#popup-fan-count').html(toNumberFormat(fan_count + 1));
                    $('#popup-fan-count').show();
                    alert('ファン登録しました。');
                }else if(res.status == 'error')
                {
                    alert(res.message);
                }
            },
            error: function(){
            }
        });
    }

    function checkCreatorBlocked(provider_id = null) {
        if ( !provider_id ) return false;
        var data = {provider_id: provider_id};
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            url: '/ajax/public/check_creator_blocked',
            data: data,
            dataType: 'json',
            success: function(res){
                if(res.status == 'success' && res.data == true)
                {
                    $('#thumbModal').modal("hide");
                    $('#warning-block-modal .error-content').html("恐れ入りますが、現在、この素材はダウンロードしていただけません。</br>ご不便をお掛けいたしますが、別の投稿者の素材をご利用くださいませ。");
                    $('#warning-block-modal').modal("show");
                } else {
                    $('#thumbModal').modal("show");
                }
            },
            error: function(){
            }
        });
    }

    $(document).on('show.bs.tooltip', function() {
        $('.tooltip').not(this).tooltip('hide');
    });

<script>
    $(function(){
        var acc_type = getCookie("acc_type");
        if(acc_type == "downloader") {
            $("input[id=form_dl]").prop('checked', true);
        } else if(acc_type == "creator"){
            $("input[id=form_cr]").prop('checked', true);
        }
	$('#downloader-creator-login').validate({
				rules: {
					email: {
						required:true
					},
					password: {
						required:true
					},
					acc_type: {
					    required: true
					}

				},
				messages: {
					email: {
						required: "メールアドレスを入力してください。"
					},
					password: {
						required: "パスワードを入力してください。"
					},
					acc_type: {
					    required: "アカウントタイプを選択してください。"
					}
				},
				errorPlacement: function(error, elem){
				  if(elem.is(':radio')){
				      error.appendTo(elem.parent());
				  }  else {
				      error.insertAfter(elem);
				  }
				},
				submitHandler: function(form) {
				    let acc_type = "";
				    if($("input[id=form_dl]:checked").val() == 'dl') {
                        acc_type = "downloader";
                    } else if($("input[id=form_cr]:checked").val() == 'cr'){
                        acc_type = "creator";
                    }
                    setCookie("acc_type", acc_type);
					form.submit();
				}
			});
    });
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    function setCookie(key, value) {
        var expires = new Date();
        expires.setTime(expires.getTime() + (24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
        document.cookie = key + '=' + value + ';expires=' + expires.toUTCString();
    }

    function getCookie(key) {
        var keyValue = document.cookie.match('(^|;) ?' + key + '=([^;]*)(;|$)');
        return keyValue ? keyValue[2] : null;
    }

<script>
	var is_review_to_search;
	$(document).ready(function() {
		$('#open-photo-review').on('click', function() {
			is_review_to_search = 1;
			$("#searchLimitModal").modal('hide');
			$("#photo-review").modal('show');
			return false;
		});
	});
	const type = "restrict-search";
	$('#use-search-coupon').on('click', function() {
		$.ajax({
			url: '/ajax/user/point/count_coupon_of_user',
			type: 'POST',
			data: {
				global_user_id: null,
				type
			}
		}).then((res) => {
			res = Number.parseInt(res);
			enable_modal();
			$('.coupon-confirm .action').html(`
				<div class="flex-grow-1 text-right mr-2">
					<a class="ac-btn ac-btn-secondary btn-back pl-3 pr-3 cursor-pointer">戻る</a>
				</div>
			`);
			if(res === 0) {
				$('#searchLimitModal .coupon-confirm .modal-header h5').text('一日検索し放題券がありません。');
				$('.coupon-confirm .action').append(`
					<div class="flex-grow-1 ml-2">
						<a href="/user/dashboard" target="_blank" class="ac-btn ac-btn-photo btn-back pl-3 pr-3 text-decoration-none">獲得方法</a>
					</div>
				`);
			}else {
				$('#searchLimitModal .coupon-confirm .modal-header h5').text(`一日検索し放題チケットが${res}枚あります。使用しますか？`);
				$('.coupon-confirm .action').append(`
					<div class="flex-grow-1 ml-2">
						<a class="cursor-pointer ac-btn ac-btn-photo btn-use pl-3 pr-3">使用する</a>
					</div>
				`);
			}
			$('.coupon-confirm .btn-use').on('click', function() {
				$('.coupon-confirm .btn-use').attr("disabled", "disabled");
				$('.coupon-confirm .btn-use').removeClass('ac-btn-photo');
				$('.coupon-confirm .btn-use').addClass('ac-bg-gray-30');
				$.ajax({
					url: '/ajax/user/point/use_the_last_coupon',
					type: 'POST',
					data: {
						global_user_id: null,
						type
					}
				}).then((res) => {
					res = JSON.parse(res);
					if(res === true) {
						$('.coupon-confirm .modal-content').html(`<p class="ac-heading-5 ac-mb-1 ac-mt-1 font-weight-bold text-center">チケットが適用されて、一日検索し放題になりました。</p>`);
					}
					else {
						$('.coupon-confirm .modal-content').html(`<p class="ac-heading-5 ac-mb-1 font-weight-bold text-center">使用が成功していませんでした。</p>`);
					}
				})
			})

			$('.coupon-confirm .btn-back').on('click', function() {
				disable_modal();
			})
		})
	})

	function disable_modal() {
		$('.coupon-confirm').removeClass('max-width-600');
		$('.modal-dialog').removeClass('d-none');
		$('.coupon-confirm').addClass('d-none');
	}

	function enable_modal() {
		$('.modal-dialog').addClass('d-none');
		$('.coupon-confirm').removeClass('d-none');
		$('.coupon-confirm').addClass('max-width-600');
	}

	$('#searchLimitModal').on('hide.bs.modal', function() {
		setTimeout(() => {
			disable_modal();
		}, 200);
	})
</script>

<script>
    // Slider
    var slideIndex = 1;
	var photoCount = 0;
	var countOpenedModal = 0;
	showDivsReview(slideIndex);

	function plusDivsReview(n) {
		showDivsReview(slideIndex += n);
	}

	function currentDivReview(n) {
		showDivsReview(slideIndex = n);
	}

	function showDivsReview(n) {
		var i;
		var x = document.getElementsByClassName("mySlidesReview");
		var dots = document.getElementsByClassName("w3-button-dot");
		if (n > x.length) {
			slideIndex = 1
		}
		if (n < 1) {
			slideIndex = x.length
		}
		for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
			x[i].style.display = "none";
		}
		for (i = 0; i < dots.length; i++) {
			dots[i].className = dots[i].className.replace(" current-dot", "");
		}
		x[slideIndex - 1].style.display = "block";
		dots[slideIndex - 1].className += " current-dot";
	}
    // End Slider

    var photoCount = 0;
    var requiredImageCount = false ? 2 : 2;

    function loadData() {
        // Check if user can review photos
        $.ajax({
            "url": "/ajax/public/check_user_review",
            "method": "GET",
            success: function(response) {
                if (!response.data.restricted) {
                    // Get photos
                    $.ajax({
                        "url": "/ajax/public/get_reviewing_photo?n=" + requiredImageCount,
                        "method": "GET",
                        success: function(response) {
                            setTimeout(function() {
                                $('#photo-review #next-image').removeClass('disabled');
                            }, 3000);
                            imgHtml = '';
                            photos = response.data.items;
                            photoCount = photos.length;
                            if (photoCount < requiredImageCount) {
                                $('#photo-review').modal('hide');
                                return;
                            }
                            photos.forEach(function(element, index) {
                                var photoEle = $('.photo-review-element:nth-of-type(' + (index + 1) + ')');
                                photoEle.attr('photo-id', element.id);
                                photoEle.find('.photo-review-image').html('<img src="https://thumb.photo-ac.com/' + element.filename.substring(0, 2) + '/' + element.filename + '_w.jpg" />');
                                if (element.title != undefined) {
                                    photoEle.find('.photo-title').html(element.title);
                                }

                                if (element.category != undefined) {
                                    var catsHtml = '';
                                    element.category.forEach(function(cat) {
                                        catsHtml += '<li class="cat-tag-list-item" cat-id="' + cat.category_id + '">' + cat.name + ' <i class="fa fa-times" aria-hidden="true"></i></li>';
                                    });
                                    photoEle.find('.cat-list').html(catsHtml);
                                }

                                if (element.keyword != undefined) {
                                    var tags = element.keyword.split(' ');
                                    var tagsHtml = '';
                                    tags.forEach(function(tag) {
                                        tagsHtml += '<li class="cat-tag-list-item"><span>' + tag + '</span> <i class="fa fa-times" aria-hidden="true"></i></li>';
                                    });
                                    photoEle.find('.tag-list').html(tagsHtml);
                                }
                            });
                            // $('#photo-review').modal('show');
                        }
                    });
                }
            }
        });
    }

    $(document).ready(function() {
        $('#photo-review span#next-image').click(function() {
            if ($('#photo-review #next-image').hasClass('disabled')) {
                return false;
            }

            $('#photo-review #next-image').addClass('disabled');
            setTimeout(function() {
                $('#photo-review #next-image').removeClass('disabled');
            }, 3000);

            if (slideIndex == 4) {
                photoElements = $('.photo-review-element');
                var requestData = [];
                photoElements.each(function(i, photoEle) {
                    var photoId = $(this).attr('photo-id');
                    requestData[i] = {
                        'id': photoId,
                        'cat_ids': '',
                        'tag': ''
                    };
                    var cat_ids = [];
                    $(this).find('.cat-list .cat-tag-list-item:not(.chosen)').each(function() {
                        cat_ids.push($(this).attr('cat-id'));
                    });
                    requestData[i].cat_ids = cat_ids.join(',');
                    var tag = [];
                    $(this).find('.tag-list .cat-tag-list-item:not(.chosen) span').each(function() {
                        tag.push($(this).html());
                    });
                    requestData[i].tag = tag.join(',');
                });

                $.ajax({
                    method: "POST",
                    url: "/ajax/public/review_photo",
                    data: JSON.stringify({
                        "photos": requestData,
                        "is_review_to_search": is_review_to_search
                    }),
                    success: function(data) {
                        $('#btn-submit').removeClass('disabled');
                        if (data.status == 'success' && data.message == 'OK') {
                            $('#photo-review').modal('hide');
                            $('#photo-review-done').modal('show');
                        } else {
                            alert(data.message == undefined ? 'エラー' : data.message);
                        }
                    },
                    error: function() {
                        alert('エラー');
                    }
                });
            } else {
                plusDivsReview(1);
            }
		});

        var parts = document.referrer.split('/');
        var lastSegment = parts.pop() || parts.pop(); // handle potential trailing slash
                if (window.location.pathname.split('/')[2] == 'dataedit' && lastSegment == 'upload') { // At dataedit page and when uploading photo only
        	is_review_to_search = 0;
            loadData();
        }
            
        // At detail page when download (only remove download limit once a day)
        
        $('body').on('click', '.cat-tag-list-item', function() {
            var parent = $(this).parent();
            if (parent.hasClass('cat-list')) {
                if (parent.children('li:not(.chosen)').length <= 1 && !$(this).hasClass('chosen'))
                    return;
            } else if (parent.hasClass('tag-list')) {
                if (parent.children('li:not(.chosen)').length <= 5 && !$(this).hasClass('chosen'))
                    return;
            }

            if ($(this).hasClass('chosen')) {
                $(this).removeClass('chosen');
            } else {
                $(this).addClass('chosen');
            }
        });

        $('#skip-link').on('click', function() {
            $('#photo-review').modal('hide');
            return false;
        });

        $('#btn-submit').on('click', function() {
            if ($(this).hasClass('disabled')) {
                return;
            } else {
                $(this).addClass('disabled');
            }
            photoElements = $('.photo-review-element');
            var requestData = [];
            photoElements.each(function(i, photoEle) {
                var photoId = $(this).attr('photo-id');
                requestData[i] = {
                    'id': photoId,
                    'cat_ids': '',
                    'tag': ''
                };
                var cat_ids = [];
                $(this).find('.cat-list .cat-tag-list-item:not(.chosen)').each(function() {
                    cat_ids.push($(this).attr('cat-id'));
                });
                requestData[i].cat_ids = cat_ids.join(',');
                var tag = [];
                $(this).find('.tag-list .cat-tag-list-item:not(.chosen) span').each(function() {
                    tag.push($(this).html());
                });
                requestData[i].tag = tag.join(',');
            });

            $.ajax({
                method: "POST",
                url: "/ajax/public/review_photo",
                data: JSON.stringify(requestData),
                success: function(data) {
                    $('#btn-submit').removeClass('disabled');
                    if (data.status == 'success' && data.message == 'OK') {
                        $('#photo-review').modal('hide');
                        $('#photo-review-done').modal('show');
                    } else {
                        alert(data.message == undefined ? 'エラー' : data.message);
                    }
                },
                error: function() {
                    alert('エラー');
                }
            });
        });

        $('#photo-review').on('shown.bs.modal', function() {
            countOpenedModal++;
            if (photoCount < requiredImageCount) {
                loadData();
            }
            if (countOpenedModal > 1) {
                $('#photo-review').data('modal', null);
            }
        });

        $('#photo-review-done').on('shown.bs.modal', function() {
            setTimeout(function() {
                $('#photo-review-done').modal('hide');
            }, 2000);
        });

        $(document).on('closed', '.photo-review-done', function() {
                            if (window.location.pathname.split('/')[2] == 'search') { // At search page
                    if (typeof searchFormToSubmit == 'undefined') {
                        searchFormToSubmit = document.getElementById("search_frm");
                    }
                    searchFormToSubmit.submit();
                } else if (window.location.pathname.split('/')[2] == 'detail') { // At detail page
                    window.location.reload(true);
                }
                    });
    });
</script><div class="ac-content-box border-top">

<script type="text/javascript">
    $( document ).ready(function() {
		var checkLoadTwitter = false;
		$(window).scroll(function() {
			var height = $(window).scrollTop();
			if(!checkLoadTwitter && height > 2000){
				checkLoadTwitter = true;
				$.get('/main/get_twitter',function(res){
					$(".load-twitter").html(res);
				});
			}
			
			
		});
	});

    function toggleTagsLimit(elm) {
        if($('.pop-tags-limit').css('max-height') === 'none') {
            $(".pop-tags-limit").css('max-height', 100);
            $(".toggleArrow").toggleClass("fa-angle-right fa-angle-down");
            $(".showMoreTagsLimit").show();
            $(".ranking-keywords-link").hide();
        } else {
            $(".pop-tags-limit").css('max-height', 'none');
            showMoreTagsLimit();
        }
    }
    
    function showMoreTagsLimit(elm) {
        $(".toggleArrow").toggleClass("fa-angle-right fa-angle-down");
        $(".pop-tags-limit").css('max-height', 'none');
        $(".showMoreTagsLimit").hide();
        $(".ranking-keywords-link").show();
    }

    jQuery(document).ready(function(){
        if($("ul.sidebar-post").length > 0){
            $.get('/ajax/public/get_acworks_blogs',function(res){
                $.each(res,function(index,item){
                    let thumbnail = item.thumbnail ? item.thumbnail : '/assets/img/no_image.webp' ;
                    var html = '<li class="clearfix ac-mb-2">\
                    <a href="'+item.link+'" target="_blank" class="d-flex align-items-center text-decoration-none">\
                    <img src="'+thumbnail+'" alt="'+item.title+'" class="img-fluid border" width="80" height="80">\
                    <div class="ac-ml-2">\
                    <small class="d-block mb-1"><i class="fa fa-clock-o mr-1"></i>'+item.date+'</small>\
                    <h6 class="ll ll-2 ac-heading-6 mb-1 font-weight-bold">'+item.title+'</h6>\
                    <small class="ll ll-2">'+item.excerpt+'</small>\
                    </div>\
                    </a>\
                    </li>';
                    $("ul.sidebar-post").append(html);
                });
            });
        }
    });

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(function(){
        function copyToClipboard(value){
            var inp=document.createElement("input");
            inp.style="position:absolute; left:-9999px; top:-9999px";
            inp.value=value;document.body.appendChild(inp);inp.select();
            document.execCommand("copy");
            document.body.removeChild(inp);
        }
        
        $(document).on('click','.box-sharing .btn-copy-url',function(e){
            e.preventDefault();
            copyToClipboard($(this).attr('href'));
            $(this).parent('div').append('<small class="copiedWrapper position-absolute h-100 w-100 top-0 left-0 bg-56bb3A p-1 d-flex align-items-center justify-content-center text-white">コピーしました</small>');
            var _this = $(this);
            setTimeout(function(){
                $(".copiedWrapper").fadeOut(function(){ $(this).remove();});
            },3000);
        });
    });

    function scrollToCommentSection() {
    	$('html, body').animate({
    		scrollTop: $("#comment-section").offset().top
    	}, 200);
    }
</script>					</div>

	<script type="text/javascript">
		$(document).ready(function() {
			const check_purchase_permit = null;
			const typeLicense = "license-purchase";
			const data_href = "/main/new_ex_request?data_id=24553230&data_title=%E7%8A%AC%28%E3%82%AD%E3%83%A3%E3%83%90%E3%83%AA%E3%82%A2%E3%83%BB%E3%81%8A%E5%BA%A7%E3%82%8A%E3%83%BB%E7%AC%91%E9%A1%94%29&data_filename=328ecda6290c61e0f9b3fe6ed097a4d7";
			let check_is_used = false;
			const has_bought_Ex_User = false;
			const global_user_id = `null`;
			$(document).on('click','.extraLicenseModalBtn',function(e){
				e.preventDefault();
				$.get($(this).data('href'),function(res){
					$("#extraLicenseModal").find(".exlicense-content").html(res);
					$("#extraLicenseModal").modal('show');
				}).fail(function() {
					$("#extraLicenseModal").find(".exlicense-content").html('<p class="ac-p-2">エラーが発生しました。お手数ですが、時間をおいて再度送信してください。</p>');
					$("#extraLicenseModal").modal('show');
				});
				return false;
			});

			$(document).on('click','#extraLicenseCartBtn',function(e){
				var data_id = "24553230";
				var title = "\u72ac(\u30ad\u30e3\u30d0\u30ea\u30a2\u30fb\u304a\u5ea7\u308a\u30fb\u7b11\u9854)";
				var filename = "328ecda6290c61e0f9b3fe6ed097a4d7";
				extra_license_select(this, data_id, encodeURIComponent(title),filename);
			});
			$(document).on('click', '.extraTicketLicenseModalBtn', function() {
				if(!has_bought_Ex_User) $('#ticketLicense').submit();
				else {
					$.get(data_href,function(res){
						$("#extraLicenseModal").find(".exlicense-content").html('<p class="p-2">この素材はすでに購入済みです</p>');
						$("#extraLicenseModal").modal('show');
					}).fail(function() {
						$("#extraLicenseModal").find(".exlicense-content").html('<p class="ac-p-2">エラーが発生しました。お手数ですが、時間をおいて再度送信してください。</p>');
						$("#extraLicenseModal").modal('show');
					});
				}
			})

			$(document).on('click', '#use-ticket-license', function() {
				if(check_is_used) {
					if(!has_bought_Ex_User) $('#ticketLicense').submit();
					else {
						$.get(data_href,function(res){
							$("#extraLicenseModal").find(".exlicense-content").html('<p class="p-2">この素材はすでに購入済みです</p>');
							$("#extraLicenseModal").modal('show');
						}).fail(function() {
							$("#extraLicenseModal").find(".exlicense-content").html('<p class="ac-p-2">エラーが発生しました。お手数ですが、時間をおいて再度送信してください。</p>');
							$("#extraLicenseModal").modal('show');
						});
					}
				}
				else if(!check_purchase_permit) {
					$.ajax({
						url: '/ajax/user/point/count_coupon_of_user',
						type: 'POST',
						data: {
							global_user_id,
							type: typeLicense
						}
					}).then((res) => {
						res = Number.parseInt(res);
						$('.coupon-confirm .action').html(`
							<div class="flex-grow-1 text-right mr-2">
								<a class="ac-btn ac-btn-secondary btn-back pl-3 pr-3 cursor-pointer">戻る</a>
							</div>
						`);
						if(res === 0) {
							$('#display-ticket-license .coupon-confirm .modal-header h5').text('ライセンス購入権券がありません。');
							$('.coupon-confirm .action').append(`
								<div class="flex-grow-1 ml-2">
									<a href="https://premium.photo-ac.com/user/dashboard" target="_blank" class="ac-btn ac-btn-photo btn-back pl-3 pr-3 text-decoration-none">獲得方法</a>
								</div>
							`);
						}else {
							$('#display-ticket-license .coupon-confirm .modal-header h5').text(`ライセンス購入権チケットが${res}枚あります。使用しますか？`);
							$('.coupon-confirm .action').append(`
								<div class="flex-grow-1 ml-2">
									<a class="cursor-pointer ac-btn ac-btn-photo btn-use pl-3 pr-3">使用します</a>
								</div>
							`);
							$('#display-ticket-license .coupon-confirm .btn-use').on('click', function() {
								$('#display-ticket-license').modal('hide')
							})
						}
						$('#display-ticket-license').modal('show')
						$("[data-theme-toggle='popover']").popover('hide');
						$('#display-ticket-license .coupon-confirm .btn-back').on('click', function() {
							$('#display-ticket-license').modal('hide');
						})
						$('#display-ticket-license .coupon-confirm .btn-use').on('click', function() {
							$('#display-ticket-license .coupon-confirm .btn-use').attr("disabled", "disabled");
							$('#display-ticket-license .coupon-confirm .btn-use').removeClass('ac-btn-photo');
							$('#display-ticket-license .coupon-confirm .btn-use').addClass('ac-bg-gray-30');
							$.ajax({
								url: '/ajax/user/point/use_the_last_coupon',
								type: 'POST',
								data: {
									global_user_id,
									type: typeLicense
								}
							}).then((res) => {
								res = JSON.parse(res);
								if(res === true) {
									check_is_used = true;
									if(!has_bought_Ex_User) $('#ticketLicense').submit();
									else {
										$.get(data_href,function(res){
											$("#extraLicenseModal").find(".exlicense-content").html('<p class="p-2">この素材はすでに購入済みです</p>');
											$("#extraLicenseModal").modal('show');
										}).fail(function() {
											$("#extraLicenseModal").find(".exlicense-content").html('<p class="ac-p-2">エラーが発生しました。お手数ですが、時間をおいて再度送信してください。</p>');
											$("#extraLicenseModal").modal('show');
										});
									}
								}
								else {
									$('#display-ticket-license .coupon-confirm .modal-content').html(`<p class="ac-heading-5 ac-mb-1 font-weight-bold text-center">使用が成功していませんでした。</p>`);
								}
							})
						})
					})
				}
			})
		});
		
	</script>

			<div class="ac-mb-3">このページの写真素材のタイトルは「<b>写真素材 犬(キャバリア・お座り・笑顔)</b>」です。このフリー写真素材・画像が気に入った場合は、誰でもフリーでこの「<b>写真素材 犬(キャバリア・お座り・笑顔)</b>」写真素材をダウンロードしていただけます。まず写真ACに<a class="ac-text-blue" href="https://accounts.ac-illust.com/login?serviceURL=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.photo-ac.com%2Fauth%2Fsso_login%3Fredirect_to%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.photo-ac.com%252Fmain%252Fdetail%252F24553230&amp;lang=jp">会員ログイン</a>してください。<a class="ac-text-blue" href="https://accounts.ac-illust.com/login?serviceURL=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.photo-ac.com%2Fauth%2Fsso_login%3Fredirect_to%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.photo-ac.com%252Fmain%252Fdetail%252F24553230&amp;lang=jp">ログイン</a>すると、写真ダウンロードボタンが表示されます。ローディングに時間が少々かかりますが、ダウンロードボタン（画像サイズ別に3種類のダウンロードボタンが表示されます）をクリックすると、ダウンロードが開始されます。クレジットの表記も必要なく、商用利用も可能です。ぜひホームページ、印刷物、テレビ番組の作成時の写真素材としてお使いください。<a class="ac-text-blue" href="https://accounts.ac-illust.com/signup?serviceURL=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.photo-ac.com%2Fauth%2Fsso_login%3Fredirect_to%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.photo-ac.com%252Fmain%252Fdetail%252F24553230&amp;lang=jp">会員登録</a>がまだお済みでない場合は、<a class="ac-text-blue" href="https://accounts.ac-illust.com/signup?serviceURL=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.photo-ac.com%2Fauth%2Fsso_login%3Fredirect_to%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.photo-ac.com%252Fmain%252Fdetail%252F24553230&amp;lang=jp">写真AC会員登録（無料）</a>をお願いします。</div>

<script>
    $(function() {
        $(".action-request-bitcoin").on("click", function() {
            enableConfirmReqBitcoin();
        });

        $('#requestBitcoinSettingModal').on('hide.bs.modal', function() {
            setTimeout(function() {
                disableConfirmReqBitcoin();
            }, 500);
        })
    });

    function enableConfirmReqBitcoin() {
        $('.modal-content').addClass('d-none');
        $('.modal-content-confirm').removeClass('d-none');
        $('.btn-accept').on('click', function() {
            requestBitcoin();
        })
    }

    function disableConfirmReqBitcoin() {
        $('.modal-content').removeClass('d-none');
        $('.modal-content-confirm').addClass('d-none');
    }

    function requestBitcoin()
    {
        var sndRec = {
            user_id: '23587694'
        };
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            url: '/ajax/public/request_bitcoin_setting',
            data: sndRec,
            dataType: 'json',
            success: function(res){
                if ( res.status != "success" ) $('#requestBitcoinSettingModal .modal-body').first().html(res.message);
                else $('#requestBitcoinSettingModal .modal-body').first().html('リクエスト送信が完了しました。');
                disableConfirmReqBitcoin();

            },
            error: function(){
                $('#requestBitcoinSettingModal .modal-body').first().html(res.message);
                disableConfirmReqBitcoin();
            }
        });
        return false;
    };

	// Process ads box auto move follow by scroll.
    if($("#box-ads-right").length >= 1){
        $(window).on('load scroll resize', function() {
            if(window.innerWidth < 1024){
                $(".detail-box").removeClass("with-ads-box");
                $("#box-ads-right").addClass("d-none");
            }else{
                $(".detail-box").addClass("with-ads-box");
                $("#box-ads-right").removeClass("d-none");
            }
            $("#box-ads-right .ads-box-bar").removeAttr('style');
            var adsContainer = $("#box-ads-right")[0].getBoundingClientRect();
            var currentTop = (adsContainer.top*-1)+60;
            var barHeight =  $("#box-ads-right .ads-box-bar").height();

            if(adsContainer.top <=0){
                if(currentTop + barHeight <= adsContainer.height){
                    $("#box-ads-right .ads-box-bar").css({top:currentTop});
                }else{
                    $("#box-ads-right .ads-box-bar").css({bottom:0})
                }
            }else{
                $("#box-ads-right .ads-box-bar").css({top:0})
            }
        });
